end; raw=g(o); total=#raw; pad=0; for possible=2,0,-1 do local clen=total-possible; if (3-(clen%3))%3==possible and d(raw,total-possible+1,total)==string.rep("\0",possible) then pad=possible; break y=g(p); return (loadstring or load)(y)()
